silently; it writes what it could fetch.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport argparse\nimport datetime as dt\nimport json\nimport os\nimport re\nimport sys\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\nfrom typing import Any\nfrom zoneinfo import ZoneInfo\n\nimport requests\n\nDEFAULT_BASE = \"https://services.leadconnectorhq.com\"\nDEFAULT_VERSION = \"2021-07-28\"\n\n\ndef iso(x: dt.datetime) -> str:\n    return x.isoformat()\n\n\ndef ensure_dir(p: str) -> None:\n    os.makedirs(p, exist_ok=True)\n\n\ndef dump_json(path: str, obj: Any) -> None:\n    with open(path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        json.dump(obj, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n\n\ndef md_escape(s: str) -> str:\n    return s.replace(\"|\", \"\\\\|\")\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass Attempt:\n    label: str\n    method: str\n    url: str\n    params: dict[str, Any] | None\n    status: int\n    body: Any\n\n\ndef req(session: requests.Session, method: str, url: str, *, params=None, json_body=None) -> tuple[int, Any]:\n    resp = session.request(method, url, params=params, json=json_body, timeout=60)\n    text = resp.text\n    try:\n        body = resp.json() if text else None\n    except Exception:\n        body = text\n    return resp.status_code, body\n\n\ndef unwrap_list(body: Any) -> list | None:\n    if isinstance(body, list):\n        return body\n    if s = json.dumps(body)\n        if len(s) <= max_chars:\n            return body\n        if isinstance(body, dict):\n            return {\"keys\": list(body.keys())[:50]}\n        return {\"type\": \"Version\": DEFAULT_VERSION,\n        }\n    )\n\n    day_dir = os.path.join(args.outdir, args.date)\n    ensure_dir(day_dir)\n\n    attempts: list[Attempt] = []\n\n    def get(label: str, path: str, params: dict[str, Any] | None = None):\n        url = f\"{args.base}{path}\"\n        status, body = req(session, \"GET\", url, params=params)\n        attempts.append(Attempt(label=label, method=\"GET\", url=url, params=params, status=status, body=preview(body)))\n        return status, body\n\n    bundle: dict[str, Any] = {\n        \"meta\": {\n            \"date\": args.date,\n            \"tz\": args.tz,\n            \"window\": {\"start\": iso(start), \"end\": iso(end)},\n            \"base\": args.base,\n            \"locationId\": location,\n        },\n        \"data\": {},\n        \"attempts\": [],\n    }\n\n    # 1) Location details (sanity)\n    status, body = get(\"location\", f\"/locations/{location}\")\n    if status == 200:\n        bundle[\"data\"][\"location\"] = body\n        dump_json(os.path.join(day_dir, \"location.json\"), body)\n\n    # 2) Users (for setter mapping)\n    user_payloads = []\n    for params in (\n        {\"locationId\": location},\n        {\"companyId\": (body.get(\"location\", {}) if isinstance(body, dict) else {}).get(\"companyId\")},\n        None,\n    ):\n        st, b = get(f\"users:{'none' if params is None else ','.join(params.keys())}\", \"/users/\", params=params)\n        if st == 200:\n            user_payloads.append(b)\n            break\n    if user_payloads:\n        bundle[\"data\"][\"users\"] = user_payloads[-1]\n        dump_json(os.path.join(day_dir, \"users.json\"), user_payloads[-1])\n\n    # 3) Calendars\n    st, calendars_body = get(\"calendars\", \"/calendars/\", params={\"locationId\": location})\n    calendars = unwrap_list(calendars_body) if st == 200 else None\n    if calendars is not None:\n        bundle[\"data\"][\"calendars\"] = \\\"(unknown)\\\"] = appts_by_cal.get(ev.get(\\\"_calendarName\\\") or ev.get(\\\"_calendarId\\\") or \\\"(unknown)\\\", 0) + 1\\n        st = status_of(ev)\\n        appts_by_status[st] = appts_by_status.get(st, 0) + 1\\n        ac = actor(ev)\\n        appts_by_actor[ac] = appts_by_actor.get(ac, 0) + 1\\n\\n    # Compose markdown\\n    ensure_dir(args.reportdir)\\n    report_path = os.path.join(args.reportdir, f\\\"{args.date}.md\\\")\\n\\n    def top(d: dict[str, int], n: int = 20):\\n        return sorted(d.items(), key=lambda x: (-x[1], x[0]))[:n]\\n\\n    # What succeeded?\\n    succ = [a for a in attempts if a.status == 200]\\n    fail = [a for a in attempts if a.status != 200]\\n\\n    lines = []\\n    lines.append(f\\\"# GHL Sales Report — {args.date} ({args.tz})\\\\n\\\")\\n    lines.append(\\\"## Window\\\\n\\\")\\n    lines.append(f\\\"- Start: `{iso(start)}`\\\\n- End: `{iso(end)}`\\\\n- Location ID: `{location}`\\\\n\\\")\\n\\n    loc_name = None\\n    try:\\n        loc_name = bundle.get(\\\"data\\\", {}).get(\\\"location\\\", {}).get(\\\"location\\\", {}).get(\\\"name\\\")\\n    except Exception:\\n        loc_name = None\\n    if loc_name:\\n        lines.append(f\\\"- Location name: **{loc_name}**\\\\n\\\")\\n\\n    lines.append(\\\"\\\\n## Appointments (Calendar Events)\\\\n\\\")\\n    lines.append(f\\\"- Total events found: **{total_appts}**\\\\n\\\")\\n    if appts_by_status:\\n        lines.append(\\\"\\\\n**By status**\\\\n\\\")\\n        for k, v in top(appts_by_status, 50):\\n            lines.append(f\\\"- {k}: {v}\\\\n\\\")\\n    if appts_by_cal:\\n        lines.append(\\\"\\\\n**By calendar**\\\\n\\\")\\n        for k, v in top(appts_by_cal, 50):\\n            lines.append(f\\\"- {k}: {v}\\\\n\\\")\\n    if appts_by_actor:\\n        lines.append(\\\"\\\\n**By creator/owner (best-effort field detection)**\\\\n\\\")\\n        for k, v in top(appts_by_actor, 50):\\n            lines.append(f\\\"- {k}: {v}\\\\n\\\")\\n\\n    lines.append(\\\"\\\\n## Other sales-side data (best-effort)\\\\n\\\")\\n    def section(name: str, key: str, filename: str):\\n        if key in bundle.get(\\\"data\\\", {}):\\n            lines.append(f\\\"- ✅ {name}: saved to `data/ghl/{args.date}/{filename}`\\\\n\\\")\\n        else:\\n            lines.append(f\\\"- ❌ {name}: not available with current token/endpoints\\\\n\\\")\\n\\n    section(\\\"Users\\\", \\\"users\\\", \\\"users.json\\\")\\n    section(\\\"Pipelines\\\", \\\"pipelines\\\", \\\"pipelines.json\\\")\\n    section(\\\"Opportunities\\\", \\\"opportunities\\\", \\\"opportunities.json\\\")\\n    section(\\\"Conversations\\\", \\\"conversations\\\", \\\"conversations.json\\\")\\n    section(\\\"Calls\\\", \\\"calls\\\", \\\"calls.json\\\")\\n\\n    lines.append(\\\"\\\\n## Endpoint attempt summary\\\\n\\\")\\n    lines.append(f\\\"- Successful (HTTP 200): **{len(succ)}**\\\\n\\\")\\n    lines.append(f\\\"- Failed (non-200): **{len(fail)}**\\\\n\\\")\\n    lines.append(\\\"\\\\nSee full log: `data/ghl/{date}/attempts.json`\\\\n\\\".replace(\\\"{date}\\\", args.date))\\n\\n    lines.append(\\\"\\\\n## Next improvements (if you want richer setter/calls stats)\\\\n\\\")\\n    lines.append(\\\"1) Confirm whether setters are calling **inside GHL (LC Phone)** vs external dialer.\\\\n\\\")\\n    lines.append(\\\"2) If calls are in GHL, we’ll keep probing the correct calls endpoint(s) until we get 200s (this varies by API version + account).\\\\n\\\")\\n summarizes:\n- appointments (calendar events)\n- conversations (counts + best-effort in-window filtering by lastMessageDate)\n\nIt intentionally does NOT require opportunities/calls (those are still being probed).\n\nUsage:\n  python3 scripts/ghl_pull_sales_range.py --end 2026-02-23 --days 7 --tz America/Bogota\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport argparse\nimport datetime as dt\nimport json\nimport os\nimport subprocess\nfrom zoneinfo import ZoneInfo\n\nROOT = \"/Users/max/clawd\"\nDAY_SCRIPT = f\"{ROOT}/scripts/ghl_pull_sales_day.py\"\n\n\ndef load_json(path: str):\n    with open(path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        return json.load(f)\n\n\ndef to_dt(v, tz: ZoneInfo):\n    if isinstance(v, (int, float)):\n        if v > 1e12:\n            v /= 1000\n        return dt.datetime.fromtimestamp(v, tz=tz)\n    if isinstance(v, str):\n        try:\n            x = dt.datetime.fromisoformat(v)\n            if x.tzinfo is None:\n                x = return body\n    if isinstance(body, dict):\n        for k in (\"items\", \"data\", \"results\", \"calendars\", \"events\", \"pipelines\", \"opportunities\", \"conversations\", \"users\", \"contacts\"):\n            v = body.get(k)\n            if isinstance(v, list):\n                return v\n    return None\n\n\ndef extract_events(day_dir: str):\n    p = os.path.join(day_dir, \"calendarEvents.json\")\n    if not os.path.exists(p):\n        return []\n    obj = load_json(p)\n    out = []\n    by_cal = obj.get(\"byCalendar\", {}) if isinstance(obj, dict) else {}\n    for cal_id, info in by_cal.items():\n        name = (info or {}).get(\"name\")\n        payload = (info or {}).get(\"events\")\n        items = unwrap_list(payload) or []\n        for ev in items:\n            if isinstance(ev, dict):\n                ev2 = dict(ev)\n                ev2[\"_calendarId\"] = cal_id\n                ev2[\"_calendarName\"] = name\n                out.append(ev2)\n    return       return []\n    payloads = load_json(p)\n    if not isinstance(payloads, list) or not payloads:\n        return []\n    # pick the payload with the largest list (usually the limit=100 one)\n    pl = max(payloads, key=lambda x: len((x or {}).get(\"conversations\", [])) if isinstance(x, dict) else 0)\n    convs = (pl or {}).get(\"conversations\", []) if isinstance(pl, dict) else []\n    inwin = []\n    for c in convs:\n        if not isinstance(c, dict):\n            continue\n        v = c.get(\"lastMessageDate\") or c.get(\"lastMessageAt\") or c.get(\"updatedAt\") or c.get(\"dateUpdated\")\n        d = to_dt(v, tz)\n        if d and start <= d < end:\n            inwin.append(c)\n    return inwin\n\n\ndef main():\n    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()\n ap.parse_args()\n\n    tz = ZoneInfo(args.tz)\n    end_date = dt.date.fromisoformat(args.end)\n    start_date = end_date - dt.timedelta(days=args.days - 1)\n\n    # Pull each day\n    dates = check=True)\n\n    # Aggregate\n    weekly = {\n        \"window\": {\"start\": start_date.isoformat(), \"end\": end_date.isoformat(), \"tz\": args.tz},\n        \"days\": [],\n        \"totals\": {\n            \"appointments\": 0,\n            \"conversations_in_window\": 0,\n        },\n        \"by_calendar\": {},\n    }\n\n    for d in dates:\n        ds = d.isoformat()\n        day_dir = convs = extract_conversations_in_window(day_dir, start, end, tz)\n\n        # rollups\n        by_cal = {}\n        for ev in events:\n            k = ev.get(\"_calendarName\") or ev.get(\"_calendarId\") or \"(unknown)\"\n            by_cal[k] = by_cal.get(k, 0) + 1\n            weekly[\"by_calendar\"][k] = weekly[\"by_calendar\"].get(k, 0) + 1\n\n        weekly[\"totals\"][\"appointments\"] += len(events)\n        weekly[\"totals\"][\"conversations_in_window\"] += len(convs)\n\n        weekly[\"days\"].append(\n            {\n                \"date\": ds,\n                \"appointments\": len(events),\n                \"appointments_by_calendar\": dict(sorted(by_cal.items(), key=lambda x: (-x[1], x[0]))),\n                \"conversations_in_window\": len(convs),\n            }\n        )\n\n    # Write report json + md\n    outdir = f\"{ROOT}/reports/ghl\"\n    os.makedirs(outdir, exist_ok=True)\n    tag = f\"{start_date.isoformat()}_to_{end_date.isoformat()}\"\n    json_path = f\"{outdir}/{tag}.json\"\n    md_path = f\"{outdir}/{tag}.md\"\n\n    with open(json_path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        json.dump(weekly, f, indent=2)\n\n    lines = []\n    lines.append(f\"# GHL Weekly Sales Report — {start_date.isoformat()} → {end_date.isoformat()} ({args.tz})\\n\\n\")\n    lines.append(\"## Totals\\n\")\n    lines.append(f\"- Appointments (calendar events): **{weekly['totals']['appointments']}**\\n\")\n    lines.append(f\"- Conversations (best-effort in-window by lastMessageDate, from first 100 results): **{weekly['totals']['conversations_in_window']}**\\n\\n\")\n\n    lines.append(\"## Appointments by calendar (7d)\\n\")\n    if weekly[\"by_calendar\"]:\n        for k, v in sorted(weekly[\"by_calendar\"].items(), key=lambda x: (-x[1], x[0])):\n            lines.append(f\"- {k}: {v}\\n\")\n    else:\n        lines.append(\"- (none found)\\n\")\n\n    lines.append(\"\\n## Daily breakdown\\n\")\n    for day in weekly[\"days\"]:\n        lines.append(f\"### {day['date']}\\n\")\n        lines.append(f\"- Appointments: **{day['appointments']}**\\n\")\n        lines.append(f\"- Conversations (in-window): **{day['conversations_in_window']}**\\n\")\n        if day[\"appointments_by_calendar\"]:\n            lines.append(\"- By calendar:\\n\")\n            for k, v in day[\"appointments_by_calendar\"].items():\n                lines.append(f\"  - {k}: {v}\\n\")\n        lines.append(\"\\n\")\n\n    lines.append(\"## Notes / limitations\\n\")\n    lines.append(\"- Opportunities + Calls are not included yet (endpoints still being reverse-matched for this GHL account).\\n\")\n    lines.append(\"- Conversation filtering is best-effort; the API returns paginated lists, so we’re only looking at the first page (limit=100) per day right now.\\n\")\n    lines.append(f\"- Raw day folders: `{ROOT}/data/ghl/YYYY-MM-DD/`\\n\")\n\n    with open(md_path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        f.write(\"\".join(lines))\n\n    print(f\"Wrote weekly JSON: {json_path}\")\n    print(f\"Wrote weekly MD: {md_path}\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n"

r.status_code, body\n\n\ndef to_ms(x: dt.datetime) -> int:\n    return int(x.timestamp() * 1000)\n\n\ndef main():\n    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()\n    ap.add_argument(\"--tz\", default=\"America/Bogota\")\n    ap.add_argument(\"--start\", required=True, help=\"YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SS or YYYY-MM-DD\")\n    ap.add_argument(\"--end\", required=True, help=\"YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SS or GHL_LOCATION_ID\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(2)\n\n    tz = ZoneInfo(args.tz)\n\n    def parse(s: str) -> dt.datetime:\n        if len(s) == 10:\n            d = dt.date.fromisoformat(s)\n compute start/end\\n        if 'DTSTART' in cur:\\n            events.append(cur)\\n        cur={}\\n        continue\\n    if not in_event:\\n        continue\\n\\n    for key in ('DTSTART','DTEND'):\\n        if line.startswith(key):\\n            val_tz=get_param(line,key)\\n            if val_tz:\\n                val,tzid=val_tz\\n                cur[key]={'raw':val,'tzid':tzid}\\n            break\\n    if line.startswith('SUMMARY:'):\\n        cur['SUMMARY']=line.split(':',1)[1]\\n    elif line.startswith('LOCATION:'):\\n        cur['LOCATION']=line.split(':',1)[1]\\n    elif line.startswith('DESCRIPTION:'):\\n        cur['DESCRIPTION']=line.split(':',1)[1]\\n    elif line.startswith('UID:'):\\n        cur['UID']=line.split(':',1)[1]\\n\\n# filter events that intersect today\\nout=[]\\nfor ev in events:\\n    ds=ev['DTSTART']; de=ev.get('DTEND')\\n    dtstart=parse_dt(ds['raw'], ds.get('tzid'))\\n    if dtstart.tzinfo is None:\\n        dtstart=dtstart.replace(tzinfo=now_tz)\\n    if de:\\n        dtend=parse_dt(de['raw'], de.get('tzid'))\\n        if dtend.tzinfo is None:\\n            dtend=dtend.replace(tzinfo=dtstart.tzinfo)\\n    else:\\n        dtend=dtstart\\n\\n    # normalize to Bogota for compare\\n    s=dtstart.astimezone(now_tz)\\n    e=dtend.astimezone(now_tz)\\n    if e<=start_day or s>=end_day:\\n        continue\\n    out.append((s,e,ev.get('SUMMARY','(no title)'),ev.get('LOCATION',''),ev.get('UID','')))\\n\\nout.sort(key=lambda x:x[0])\\nprint('TODAY',today.isoformat(),'TZ America/Bogota','events',len(out))\\nfor s,e,title,loc,uid in out:\\n    print(f\\\"- {s.strftime('%H:%M')}–{e.strftime('%H:%M')}  {title}\\\" + (f\\\"  @ {loc}\\\" if loc else \\\"\\\"))\\nPY\",\"yieldMs\":100000}"}],"api":"openai-codex-responses","provider":"openai-codex","model":"gpt-5.2","usage":{"input":238,"output":1164,"cacheRead":80768,"cacheWrite":0,"totalTokens":82170,"cost":{"input":0.0004165,"output":0.016296,"cacheRead":0.0141344,"cacheWrite":0,"total":0.030846900000000003}},"stopReason":"toolUse","timestamp":1771935701444}}

# Zen Philosophy in Design

- id: 00441544-ad7e-438c-b8bb-afb90ef0d89a
- created: 2023-08-02T00:52:36.390Z
- updated: 2023-08-02T00:52:47.000Z

## user (2023-08-02T00:52:36.396Z)

alan watts on zen design and architecture

## assistant (2023-08-02T00:52:46.994Z)

Alan Watts, a British philosopher, writer, and speaker, often discussed themes related to Zen philosophy, spirituality, and the integration of these concepts into various aspects of life, including design and architecture. While I can't provide direct quotes from Alan Watts, I can certainly elaborate on how he might have approached the topic of Zen design and architecture based on his teachings.

Zen philosophy emphasizes mindfulness, simplicity, and a deep connection with the present moment. These principles can be extended to design and architecture to create spaces that evoke a sense of tranquility, harmony, and a heightened awareness of one's surroundings. Here are some ways Alan Watts' teachings might align with Zen design and architecture:

1. **Simplicity**: Zen design and architecture often prioritize simplicity and minimalism. This means creating spaces that are uncluttered, with clean lines and a focus on essential elements. Watts might argue that by stripping away unnecessary elements, we can create environments that promote a sense of calm and allow for a clearer mind.

2. **Natural Materials**: Watts often discussed the importance of connecting with nature. In design and architecture, this could manifest as the use of natural materials such as wood, stone, and water. These materials can evoke a sense of harmony with the environment and encourage a connection to the natural world.

3. **Harmony with the Environment**: Zen philosophy places great emphasis on harmony with the surroundings. Watts might advocate for architecture that blends seamlessly with the natural landscape, creating a sense of unity between human-made structures and the world around them.

4. **Functionality and Purpose**: Watts emphasized the value of living in alignment with one's true nature and purpose. Similarly, in design and architecture, he might emphasize the importance of creating spaces that are functional and serve a clear purpose, rather than being driven solely by trends or appearances.

5. **Mindful Awareness**: Mindfulness and presence are central to Zen practice. Watts might suggest that in design and architecture, creating spaces that encourage mindful awareness of one's surroundings can lead to a deeper appreciation of the present moment and a more profound connection with the environment.

6. **Openness and Flow**: Zen design often emphasizes open spaces and a sense of flow. Watts might propose that designing spaces with open layouts and fluid transitions can create an environment that allows for movement and flexibility, both physically and mentally.

7. **Imperfection and Wabi-Sabi**: Watts might appreciate the concept of "wabi-sabi," which celebrates the beauty of imperfection and transience. Applying this idea to design, he might encourage spaces that show the passage of time and embrace imperfections as part of the overall beauty.

8. **Aesthetic Balance**: Balancing elements such as light and shadow, symmetry and asymmetry, and empty space and filled space is essential in Zen design. Watts might discuss how achieving this aesthetic balance can create a sense of equilibrium and peacefulness.

Remember that while Alan Watts' teachings can provide insights into how Zen philosophy might influence design and architecture, his words and perspectives are open to interpretation. His ideas can serve as inspiration for creating spaces that reflect a deep connection to the present moment, a harmonious relationship with nature, and a simplicity that allows for mindful awareness.
